[32m+[m[32m  # This script is a way to set up or update your development environment automatically.[m[m

[32m+[m[32m  # Add necessary setup steps to this file.[m[m

[32m+[m[32m  puts '== Installing dependencies =='[m[m
[32m+[m[32m  system! 'gem install bundler --conservative'[m[m
[32m+[m[32m  system('bundle check') || system!('bundle install')[m[m
[32m+[m[m
[32m+[m[32m  # Install JavaScript dependencies[m[m
[32m+[m[32m  system! 'bin/yarn'[m[m
[32m+[m[m
[32m+[m[32m  # puts "\n== Copying sample files =="[m[m
[32m+[m[32m  # unless File.exist?('config/database.yml')[m[m
[32m+[m[32m  #   FileUtils.cp 'config/database.yml.sample', 'config/database.yml'[m[m
[32m+[m[32m  # end[m[m
[32m+[m[m
[32m+[m[32m  puts "\n== Preparing database =="[m[m
[32m+[m[32m  system! 'bin/rails db:prepare'[m[m
[32m+[m[m
[32m+[m[32m  puts "\n== Removing old logs and tempfiles =="[m[m
[32m+[m[32m  system! 'bin/rails log:clear tmp:clear'[m[m
[32m+[m[m
[32m+[m[32m  puts "\n== Restarting application server =="[m[m
[32m+[m[32m  system! 'bin/rails restart'[m[m

[32m+[m[32m#!/usr/bin/env ruby[m[m
[32m+[m[32mAPP_ROOT = File.expand_path('..', __dir__)[m[m
[32m+[m[32mDir.chdir(APP_ROOT) do[m[m
[32m+[m[32m  yarn = ENV["PATH"].split(File::PATH_SEPARATOR).[m[m
[32m+[m[32m    select { |dir| File.expand_path(dir) != __dir__ }.[m[m
[32m+[m[32m    product(["yarn", "yarn.cmd", "yarn.ps1"]).[m[m
[32m+[m[32m    map { |dir, file| File.expand_path(file, dir) }.[m[m
[32m+[m[32m    find { |file| File.executable?(file) }[m[m
[32m+[m[m
[32m+[m[32m  if yarn[m[m
[32m+[m[32m    exec yarn, *ARGV[m[m
[32m+[m[32m  else[m[m
[32m+[m[32m    $stderr.puts "Yarn executable was not detected in the system."[m[m
[32m+[m[32m    $stderr.puts "Download Yarn at https://yarnpkg.com/en/docs/install"[m[m
[32m+[m[32m    exit 1[m[m
[32m+[m[32m  end[m[m
[32m+[m[32mend[m[m

[32m+[m[32m#[m[m

[32m+[m[32m#[m[m

[32m+[m[32m#[m[m

[32m+[m[32m# the default I18n backend:[m[m
[32m+[m[32m#[m[m
[32m+[m[32m# true, false, on, off, yes, no[m[m
[32m+[m[32m#[m[m

[32m+[m[32m#[m[m
[32m+[m[32m# en:[m[m
[32m+[m[32m#   'true': 'foo'[m[m
[32m+[m[32m#[m[m

[32m+[m[32m# Puma can serve each request in a thread from an internal thread pool.[m[m
[32m+[m[32m# The `threads` method setting takes two numbers: a minimum and maximum.[m[m
[32m+[m[32m# Any libraries that use thread pools should be configured to match[m[m
[32m+[m[32m# the maximum value specified for Puma. Default is set to 5 threads for minimum[m[m
[32m+[m[32m# and maximum; this matches the default thread size of Active Record.[m[m
[32m+[m[32m#[m[m
[32m+[m[32mmax_threads_count = ENV.fetch("RAILS_MAX_THREADS") { 5 }[m[m
[32m+[m[32mmin_threads_count = ENV.fetch("RAILS_MIN_THREADS") { max_threads_count }[m[m
:[K[K[32m+[m[32mthreads min_threads_count, max_threads_count[m[m
[32m+[m[m
[32m+[m[32m# Specifies the `worker_timeout` threshold that Puma will use to wait before[m[m
[32m+[m[32m# terminating a worker in development environments.[m[m
[32m+[m[32m#[m[m
[32m+[m[32mworker_timeout 3600 if ENV.fetch("RAILS_ENV", "development") == "development"[m[m
[32m+[m[m
[32m+[m[32m# Specifies the `port` that Puma will listen on to receive requests; default is 3000.[m[m
[32m+[m[32m#[m[m
[32m+[m[32mport ENV.fetch("PORT") { 3000 }[m[m
[32m+[m[m
[32m+[m[32m# Specifies the `environment` that Puma will run in.[m[m
[32m+[m[32m#[m[m
[32m+[m[32menvironment ENV.fetch("RAILS_ENV") { "development" }[m[m
[32m+[m[m
[32m+[m[32m# Specifies the `pidfile` that Puma will use.[m[m
[32m+[m[32mpidfile ENV.fetch("PIDFILE") { "tmp/pids/server.pid" }[m[m
[32m+[m[m
[32m+[m[32m# Specifies the number of `workers` to boot in clustered mode.[m[m
[32m+[m[32m# Workers are forked web server processes. If using threads and workers together[m[m
[32m+[m[32m# the concurrency of the application would be max `threads` * `workers`.[m[m
[32m+[m[32m# Workers do not work on JRuby or Windows (both of which do not support[m[m
[32m+[m[32m# processes).[m[m
[32m+[m[32m#[m[m
[32m+[m[32m# workers ENV.fetch("WEB_CONCURRENCY") { 2 }[m[m
[32m+[m[m
[32m+[m[32m# Use the `preload_app!` method when specifying a `workers` number.[m[m
[32m+[m[32m# This directive tells Puma to first boot the application and load code[m[m
[32m+[m[32m# before forking the application. This takes advantage of Copy On Write[m[m
[32m+[m[32m# process behavior so workers use less memory.[m[m
[32m+[m[32m#[m[m
[32m+[m[32m# preload_app![m[m
[32m+[m[m
[32m+[m[32m# Allow puma to be restarted by `rails restart` command.[m[m
[32m+[m[32mplugin :tmp_restart[m[m
